srilanka ne ek bhi match nahin jeeta he or vah ank talika main sabase neeche he
 Despite this defeat, India's hopes of reaching the final of the Asia Cup are alive
 bharat ko apana aakhri lig muqabla Pakistan has to play and to maintain this expectation, they will have to win this match
 bhartiya team yadi pakistan se haar jaati he or bangladesh kii team agle mukaable main srilanka ko haraa detii he to is surat main bangladesh kii team kaa final kaa tikat pakkaa ho jayega
 But if the Sri Lankan team defeats Bangladesh by bonus points and India loses to Pakistan then in that case the Sri Lankan team will reach the final
 srilankai team agar bagaiyr bonus ank ke bangladesh ko haraati he to is paristhiti main bharat, bangladesh or srilanka kii tiimon ke chaar-chaar ank rahenge or phir ran ausat ke hisaab se awwal rahane vaali team ko final main jane kaa mauka milegaa
 Nonetheless, Tamim Iqbal, Zahurul Islam, former captain Shakib Al Hasan, Nasir Hussain and captain Mushfiqur Rahman played a combined role in Bangladesh's victory
 ikbaal ne 70, islam ne 53, shaakib ne 49, hossain ne 54 or captain rahim ne aakhri overon main 25 gendon par teen chaukon or teen chhakkon kii madad se dhuandhar 46 ran banaae
 Shakib Al Hasan was named Man of the Match for his outstanding performance
 bangladesh kii jeet ke saath hi puure stadium main jashn kaa maahaul rahaa
 Earlier, with the help of Sachin Tendulkar's 100th century and half-centuries from Virat Kohli and Suresh Raina, the Indian team set a target of 290 runs against Bangladesh
 test maichon main 51 or ekadivasiy maichon main 49 shatak lagane vaale sachin kii yagadar pari kii badaulat bhartiya team ne toss haarane ke baad pehle ballebaaji karte hue nirdhaarit 50 overon main paanch wicket par 289 ran banaae
 Captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni returned unbeaten on 17 and Ravindra Jadeja on four runs
 sachin 147 gendon par 12 chaukon or ek chakke kii madad se 114 ran banaakar out hue
 Kohli contributed 66 and Raina contributed 51 runs
 bharat ne 25 ran ke kul yoga par gautam gambheer kaa wicket ganvaaya tha
 Gambhir was dismissed by Saiful Islam
 vah 16 gendon par ek chauke kii madad se 11 ran bana sake
 After this Sachin and Kohli added 148 runs for the second wicket
 kohli kaa wicket 173 ranon ke kul yoga par gira
 Kohli hit five fours in his 82-ball innings
 kohli ke vidaa hone ke baad raina ne 38 gendon kaa saamana karte hue paanch chauke or do chakke lagaae
 Raina and Sachin added 86 runs for the third wicket
 isi saajhedaari ke dauraan sachin ne apane kariyar kaa 100waan shatak puraa kiya
 Sachin, who has been active in international cricket for 21 years, achieved this with a single off Saqib Al Hasan
 sachin ne apni 138 gendon kii pari main 10 chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Sachin scored his 99th international century against South Africa in Nagpur during the World Cup on March 12 last year
 iske baad 100wein shatak ke liye sachin ko ek varsh se adhik samay tak intjaar karnaa padaa
 Sachin has scored 15470 runs in 188 Tests for India
 isamen 51 shatak or 65 ardhshtak shaamil hai jabaki 462 ekadivasiy maichon main sachin ke balle se 49 shatak or 18374 ran nikle hai
 The comments 18 disambar, 1989 main apane kariyar kaa pehla ekadivasiy match khilne vaale sachin ne 462 maichon kii 451 pariyon main 41 baar naabad rahete hue 44
 Has scored at an average of 64
 unke naam 95 ardhshtak bhi darj hai
 Sachin, one of the greatest batsmen of all time, is the first batsman to score centuries in international matches
 unke naam sarvaadhik test tathaa ekadivasiy shatak ke alaava test tathaa ekadivasiy maichon main sabase adhik ran banane kaa ricard he
 India had challenged 290 runs to win in front of Bangladesh, which was won by the Bangladesh batsmen at the loss of five wickets with four balls remaining
 bangladesh ke ballebaajon ke aage bhartiya gendbaaj bebas najar aae
 The entire team contributed to Bangladesh's victory
 uski ore se teen ballebaajon ne ardhshtak lagaae jabaki do thode hi antar se isse chook gaye or bharat ko duusari baar haraakar cricket itihaas kaa ek or bada ulatpher kiya
 Bangladesh had earlier defeated India in the 2007 World Cup
 bangladesh se mili haar ke baavjood bhartiya team chaar ankon ke saath duusare sthaan par he
 Although Bangladesh also have four points, they are ranked third in terms of run average
 srilanka ne ek bhi match nahin jeeta he or vah ank talika main sabase neeche he

 But if the Sri Lankan team defeats Bangladesh by bonus points and India loses to Pakistan then in that case the Sri Lankan team will reach the final
 srilankai team agar bagaiyr bonus ank ke bangladesh ko haraati he to is paristhiti main bharat, bangladesh or srilanka kii tiimon ke chaar-chaar ank rahenge or phir ran ausat ke hisaab se awwal rahane vaali team ko final main jane kaa mauka milegaa

 haalanki bangladesh ke bhi chaar hi ank he lekin ran ausat ke hisaab se use teesraa sthaan mila he
 Sri Lanka have not won a single match and are at the bottom of the points table
 is haar ke baavjood asia cap ke final main pahunchane kii bharat kii ummiden jinda he
 India got its last league match pakistan se khelnaa he or is ummid ko banaae rakhane ke liye use is match ko har haal main jeetna hoga
 If the Indian team loses to Pakistan and the Bangladesh team defeats Sri Lanka in the next match, then the Bangladesh team's final ticket will be confirmed in this case
 lekin yadi srilankai team bangladesh ko bonus ankon se haraa detii he or bharat pakistan se haar jaataa he to is surat main srilankai team final main pahunch jaaegi
 If the Sri Lankan team beat Bangladesh without bonus points, then India, Bangladesh and Sri Lanka will have four points each in this situation and then the team topping the run average will get a chance to go to the final
 baharhaal, bangladesh kii jeet main tameem ikbaal, jahurul islam, purv captain shaakib al hasan, nasir hossain or captain mushafikur rahamaan ne sanyukt bhoomika nibhaai
 Iqbal scored 70, Islam 53, Shakib 49, Hussain 54 and captain Rahim scored 46 off 25 balls in the last over with the help of three fours and three sixes
 shaakib al hasan ko unke shandaar pradarshan ke liye main of da match kaa khitaab diya gaya
 There was a festive atmosphere throughout the stadium with the victory of Bangladesh
 isse pehle, sachin tendulkar ke kariyar ke 100wein shatak or viraat kohli tathaa suraish raina ke ardhshtakon kii madad se bhartiya team ne bangladesh ke saamne 290 ranon kaa lakshya rakhaa tha
 Sachin, who scored 51 centuries in Tests and 49 in odis, helped the Indian team score 289 for five in the allotted 50 overs, batting first after losing the toss
 captain mahendra singh dhoni 17 or rabindra jadeja chaar ran par naabad laute
 Sachin got out for 147 off 147 balls with the help of 12 fours and a six
 kohli ne 66 or raina ne 51 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 India lost the wicket of Gautam Gambhir for a total of 25 runs
 gambheer ko saful islam ne out kiya
 He could score 11 runs off 16 balls with the help of a four
 iske baad sachin or kohli ne duusare wicket ke liye 148 ran jode
 Kohli's wicket fell at a total of 173 runs
 kohli ne apni 82 gendon kii pari main paanch chauke lagaae
 After Kohli's departure, Raina faced 38 balls and hit five fours and two sixes
 raina or sachin ne tisare wicket ke liye 86 ran jode
 During this partnership, Sachin completed the 100th century of his career
 21 saal se antarrashtiya cricket main sakriy sachin ne saaqib al hasan kii gend par ek ran lene ke saath yah mukaam hasil kiya
 Sachin hit 10 fours and a six in his 138-ball innings
 sachin ne apana 99waan antarrashtriya shatak beete saal 12 march ko vishwa cap ke dauraan nagpur main dakshin africa ke khilaaf lagaaya tha
 After this, Sachin had to wait for more than a year for the 100th century
 sachin ne bharat ke liye 188 test maichon main 15470 ran banaae hai
 It includes 51 centuries and 65 fifties, while in 462 odis, Sachin's bat has produced 49 centuries and 18374 runs
 tippaniyan Sachin, who played the first ODI of his career on 18 December 1989, was 44 not out 41 times in 451 innings of 462 matches
 64 ke ausat se ran banaae hai
 Their names are also recorded in 95 fifties
 sarvakalik mahaan ballebaajon main shumaar sachin antarrashtriya maichon main shatakon kaa shatak lagane vaale pehle ballebaaj hai

 The month of Jyeshtha is the third month in the Hindu calendar
 is maheene main surya atyant taaqatvar hota he, isliye garmi bhi zyada hoti he
 This month is called Jyeshtha because of the sun's eldership
 jyeshtha nakshatra ke kaaran bhi is maah ko jyeshtha kaha jaataa he
 Relation of religion has been linked to water in this month, so that water can be conserved
 is maas main surya or varun dev kii upasna vishesh faldaayi hoti he
 This time the first month will be from May 19 to June 17
 kaise padaa jyeshtha maheene kaa naam?jyeshtha kaa maheenaa baishakh ke maheene ke baad aata he
 Talking about the English calendar, this month always comes in the months of June and May only
 mana jaataa he ki jyeshtha poornima ke din hi chandramaa jyeshtha nakshatra main hota he
 Hence this month is named Jyeshtha
 jyeshtha maas kaa vaigyanik mahatv kya he?- is maah main vaataavaran or sharir main jal kaa str girane lagata he
 Therefore, proper and adequate use of water should be done
 - san stroke or khan paan kii bimariyon se bachaav aavashyak he
 - Use of green vegetables, sattu, water fruits is beneficial in this month
 - is maheene main dopaher kaa vishram karnaa bhi laabhadaayak hota he
 What is the glory of Jyeshtha Tuesday? - Hanuman ji is specially worshiped on Tuesday of Jyeshtha
 - is din hanuman ji ko tulsi dal kii maala arpit kii jaati he
 Also, pudding is offered as an offering to puri or sweet things
 - iske baad unki stuti karen
 - Distribute pudding and water to the poor
 - aisa karne se mangal sambandhi har samasya kaa nidaan ho jayega

 to khadey rahane se calories kaise kam hoti he
 According to a report by the American Council, a person who weighs 68 kg can lose 114 calories in one hour or 912 calories in eight hours
 vahiin singhl kaa kahana he, 'main suzav duungaa ki khadey rahane kii kshamta dhire-dhire vakt ke saath aati he or ant main chaar ghante tak khadey rahane kii kshamta aapke swasthya ko laabh degi
 ' lekin sabase pehle khadey rahane ke sahi tareeke ko siikhnaa jaruri he
 Singhal suggested, 'relax your shoulders and back when you are standing, keep your head straight, try to keep your chest out and stand inside the abdomen, straight and right
 ' Ritika Samadadar of Max Super Specialty Hospital in New Delhi says, "it has always been suggested that sitting is less of calories than standing more than sitting
 ' Samadar explained, 'there is a need for a slight change in the ability to walk, in this you can walk while talking on your smartphone and you can talk by shaking your hand during a phone conversation
 ' He also suggested that if you get up from your seat every half hour and stand on your feet in a small change, then you will be more healthy and it will also reduce your weight
 iske saath hi aap swasth bhojan karen

 The possibility of becoming a cyclone in the Bay of Bengal has deepened
 mausam vibhaag ke mutabik 14 may ko srilanka ke paas bengal kii khadi main ek kam dabaav kaa kshetra ban jayega
 Due to this, there is a possibility of winds in the sea near Tamil Nadu at a speed of 30 to 40 km per hour
 kam dabaav kaa kshetra 16 may tak or zyada taqatvar hokar depressant main tabdeel ho jayega
 Advice to fishermen not to go to sea, this will start the monsoon rain in Andaman and Nicobar
 wedar system ke depressant banane ke baad ye system or zyada taqatvar ho jayega, jisase ise cyclone main tabdeel hone kii khaasi sambhaavna he
 In this context, the Meteorological Department has advised fishermen of Tamil Nadu not to venture into the sea
 tamilnadu main joardaar barish kii sambhaavnamausam vibhaag kaa kahana he ki srilanka ke aasapaasmansooni hawaonka silsilaa jald hi shuru ho jayega
 Monsoon winds will become more powerful in the Bay of Bengal
 isse barish ko taras rahe andaman nicobar main jhamajham barish kaa daur shuru ho jayega
 With this, the monsoon will knock till 16th or 17th in India
 mausam vibhaag kaa anumaan he ki bengal kii khadi main banane ja rahe is wedar system se tamilnadu main 16 taarikh ko joardaar barish kii sambhaavna he
 The special thing is that votes are being cast for the assembly elections in Tamil Nadu on 16 May
 chakravaati tufaan kaa bhi khatramausam vibhaag kaa anumaan he kibengal kii khadimen bana wedar system tamilnadu kii ore badhegaa
 With this, its strength will increase and it can turn into a cyclone
 cyclone banane ke baad tamilnadu or andhra pradesh ke tateey ilaakon main joardaar barish kaa silsilaa shuru ho jayega
 According to the weather model shown so far, after the cyclone is formed, this cyclonic storm will cross the coast between Andhra Pradesh and Tamil Nadu around 19 May
 haalanki ye shuruaati jaankaree he isse agle 48 ghanton main tej badlaav ho saktaa he

 In the decade of the Bombay capital (now Mumbai) in the capital of Maharashtra, a man working in a newspaper started writing the new destiny of Maharashtra
 Later, the world came to be known as Bala Saheb Thackeray
 maharashtra main satta chaahe kisi bhi party kii rahi ho lekin vahaan hukumat hameshaa bal thakare kii hi rahi jiske ijaajat ke bina vahaan kisi sarkaar ke liye ek patta tak hilaa paanaa asambhav sa tha

 inamen ek unka betaa to doosraa unka bhatija tha

 Uddhav Thackeray has reached the top of Maharashtra politics today and will be sworn in as the Chief Minister of the state in the coming 24 hours
 vahiin duusari taraf chachaa bal thakare se baghawat kar apni nai party maharashtra navnirmaan sena banane vaale vaale bhattije raaj thakare maharashtra kii raajnneeti ke nepathy main ja chuke hai
 While Uddhav Thackeray was leaving political legacy to follow his photography passions, on the other hand, other parties in Maharashtra including Shiv Sena started feeling nephew Raj Thackeray as Bal Thackeray's political heir
 raaj thakare ke bolne se lekar chalane tak kaa andaaj apane chachaa bal thakare se miltaa tha isliye log unhen bal thakare kii viraasat ke vaaris ke taur par dekhne lage the
 Interestingly, Raj Thackeray is also very fond of making cartoons like Bal Thackeray
 chachaa bal thakare ke har faisle main unki parchaai kii tarah saath khadey rahane vaale raaj thakare ko jab yah pataa chalaa ki chachaa unki jagah apane bete uddhav thakare ko party kii kaman or raajnneetik viraasat saunpna chaahate hai to donon ke bich matbhed shuru ho gaye
 While Bal Thackeray was in favor of handing over his political legacy to Uddhav, Raj Thackeray wanted his control over the Shiv Sena party
 party banaai lekin kaam na aiuddhav thakare ke party pramukh banane ke thode dinon baad hi tikat bantwaare main manachaaha hissaa nahin milane or satta sangharsh kii vajah se aakhirakar raaj thakare ne khud ko shivasena se alag karte hue saal 2006 main apni nai party maharashtra navnirmaan sena kaa gathan kar liya
 In 2008, two years after forming the party, Raj Thackeray's party started airing the politics and regionalism of the Marathas
 maharashtra se uttar bharatiyon ko baahar karne kii maang ko lekar sadakon par utar aae
 During this period, violence took place against North Indians in most cities from Mumbai to Maharashtra, in which the names of Raj Thackeray's party workers came out
 raaj thakare maharashtra main uttar bharatiyon kii naukariyon ke khilaaf andolan chalaane lage
 On the other hand, under the leadership of Uddhav Thackeray, the Shiv Sena started moving slowly with the BJP, an ally of his father's time, and the Shiv Sena continued its expansion from Delhi to Maharashtra
 nafrat haara, uttar bharatiyon ne thukraayasaal 2006 main nai party banane ke thik teen saal baad 2009 main jab maharashtra main vidhansabha chunaav hue to raaj thakare kii party ko 13 siton par jeet mili
 Thackeray's party won most of the seats where the number of Marathi voters was more and he did not like North Indians
 isse raaj thakare ko laga ki uttar bharatiyon kaa virodh karnaa or marathaon kii asmita kii baat karnaa unhen maharashtra kii raajnneeti main sthapit kar degaa
 After this, he constantly started insulting and provoking things against North Indians
 saal 2008 main chhath puja ko lekar die unke vivaadit bayaan ne kaaphi tool pakadaa jisaki vajah se unhen cese kaa bhi saamana karnaa padaa
 After the statement about Chhath Puja, anger started raging against him in the North Indians, whose direct loss was to Raj Thackeray's party from the local body elections to the assembly elections
 2009 vidhansabha chunaav ke baad raaj thakare kaa yah daanv ulta padana shuru ho gaya or unki nafrat bhari raajnneeti ko vahaan ke logon ne dhire-dhire asweekaar karnaa shuru kar diya
 Raj Thackeray's political downfall started from here
 saal 2012 ke biemasi chunaav main jahaan raaj thakare kii party ko 27 siten mili thi vahiin 2017 ke chunaav main unhen sirf 1 seat par jeet mili
 In the civic elections of Thane, Kalyan Ullas Nagar, Pune, Nashik, Nagpur, Malegaon, Jalgaon, Sangli, Raj Thackeray's party suffered a heavy defeat in 2017 compared to 2012
 kai jagah to unki party kaa khaataa tak nahin khulaa
 Raj Thackeray also came in support after seeing the wave of the then Prime Ministerial candidate Narendra Modi when first the fans then the critics were going to hold the Lok Sabha elections in the country in 2014
 raaj thakare ko laga ki bijepi ke kareeb jane par vah maharashtra main shivasena kaa vikalp ban sakate hai lekin aisa kuch nahin hua
 After the election year, Raj Thackeray, who used to be an admirer of PM Modi, became a critic of him, who also went to BJP supporters in Maharashtra
 maharashtra main saal 2014 main hue vidhansabha chunaav main raaj thakare kii party manase ne vidhansabha kii 288 main se 220 siton par apane ummidavaar utaare or unhen karaari haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 His party could win only one seat
 jabaki usee chunaav main shivasena ne 63 siton par shandaar jeet darj kii or maharashtra kii sarkaar main bijepi kii sahyogi party ban gai
 Raj Thackeray unofficially started an alliance with the Congress before the 2019 Maharashtra Assembly elections, but the Congress also withdrew from the MNS for fear of losing its vote bank due to his political background
 
 haalanki pehle raaj thakare ne elaan kiya ki wo rajya ke 100 siton par apane ummidavaar utaarenge lekin baad main unhone loksabhaa chunaav kii tarah vidhansabha chunaav se bhi kinaaraa kar liya
 Like the Lok Sabha elections from the BJP, the Congress and the NCP, the Shiv Sena performed better than expected in the 2019 Maharashtra Assembly elections
 bijepi ne jahaan 105 siton par jeet darj kii vahiin shivasena ne endie gathbandhan main rahete hue 56 siton par jeet darj kii or uske baad maharashtra main bijepi ke saamne dhai-dhai saal ke siem pad ko lekar shart rakh di
 When the BJP flatly refused to share the cm's post, the Shiv Sena led by Uddhav Thackeray, along with the Congress and NCP, found a way to form the government and form the CM of its own party
 kareeb ek maheene ke siyaasi daanvpench or uthapatak ke baad aakhirkaar shivasena isamen safal ho gai or ab guuruuvaar ko uddhav thakare maharashtra ke nae mukhyamantri ke taur par shapath lenge vahiin raaj thakare aaj kahaan hai or kya kar rahe hai isaki kisi ko koi khabar nahin he

 is film seharshvardhan kapooror sayaami kher apana kariyar shuru karne ja rahe hai

 yah bhavyarajasthani shadihai or is seqvence ke liye sayaani ne paaramparik rajasthani poshaak pahani he, jiskaa vajan 18 kilogram he or ise sabyasachi ne dizin kiya he
